NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

In accordance with the section 485 of the Companies Act, 1956 the General Notice is hereby given having
passed the following resolution at the Extra Ordinary General Meeting held on 20.06.2016.
“Resolve that in pursuance to Section 484 (1) (b) of the Companies Act, 1956 and other applicable
provisions and Rules made thereunder, the company be and is hereby wound up voluntarily”.
The above resolution was passed unanimously by its members.
Sivakasi,
24th June 2016.

YENNARKAY R RAJARATHNAM RAVINDRAN,
Chairman of the Meeting.

My Adopted son James, under the care of M. Rajan of Zeal Charitable Trust, Chennai, born on
23rd October 2001, has been adopted by me as my child on 10th May 2016 vide registered adoption deed bearing
No 65/2016. By this he possesses all the rights of a son, and shall reside with me in my address No.3, 18th Cross
Street, Kakilanchavadi, Sanatorium, Chrompet, Chennai-47. As I have taken him as my son, I got him converted
Hinduism on 20th June 2016 and shall henceforth be known as R. SAI DHAKSHAN.
Chennai,
24th June 2016.

R.P. RAJAGOPAL,
(Adoptive Father.)
